Roman;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">BURLINGTON, MA, and PLANO, TX (April 29, 2020) - Keurig Dr Pepper (NYSE: KDP) announced today that its Board of Directors has declared a regular quarterly cash dividend of $0.15 per share, payable in U.S. dollars, on the Company&#8217;s common stock. The regular quarterly dividend will be paid on July 17, 2020 to shareholders of record on July 3, 2020.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">ABOUT KEURIG DR PEPPER </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">Keurig Dr Pepper (KDP) is a leading beverage company in North America, with annual revenue in excess of $11 billion and nearly 26,000 employees. KDP holds leadership positions in soft drinks, specialty coffee and tea, water, juice and juice drinks and mixers, and markets the #1 single serve coffee brewing system in the U.S. and Canada. The Company&#8217;s portfolio of more than 125 owned, licensed and partner brands is designed to satisfy virtually any consumer need, any time, and includes Keurig&#174;, Dr Pepper&#174;, Green Mountain Coffee Roasters&#174;, Canada Dry&#174;, Snapple&#174;, Bai&#174;, Mott's&#174;, CORE&#174; and The Original Donut Shop&#174;. Through its powerful sales and distribution network, KDP can deliver its portfolio of hot and cold beverages to nearly every point of purchase for consumers.  The Company is committed to sourcing, producing and distributing its beverages responsibly through its Drink Well. Do Good. corporate responsibility platform, including efforts around circular packaging, efficient natural resource use and supply chain sustainability.  For more information, visit, </font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;color:#0000ff;text-decoration:underline;">www.keurigdrpepper.com</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div><br></div><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Arial;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div></div>	</div></body>
